NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
I, K.G. Ravisankar, Biological son of K.K. Gandhi Raja, residing at 307/298, Dharmaraja Big Street, Palayapalayam,
Rajapalayam, Virudhunagar-626 117, by way of this Public Notice, I inform that Thiru M.M. Regupathy Raja has legally
adopted me as his son on 2nd September 1993, by way a registered deed No. 248 of 3rd September 1993 on the file
the District Registrar of RAJAPALAYAM TALUK, VIRUDHUNAGAR DISTRICT. My adopted father M.M. Regupathy Raja
Passed away on 24th October 2007. Here after I shall be known as M.R. RAVISANKAR RAJA.
Virudhunagar,
28th February 2011.

K.G. RAVISANKAR

FORM No. 155
[See rule 329]
Member’s Voluntary Winding-up
MERCURY FILAMENTS PRIVATE LIMITED
(Registered Office address: 18/4, Jawahar Street, R.V. Puram, Nagercoil-629 001)
Notice convening final meeting
Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 of the Companies Act, 1956 that a general meeting of the members of
the above named company will be held at the Registered Office of the Company situated at 18/4, Jawahar Street,
R.V. Puram, Nagercoil-629 001 on Monday, the 11th day of April 2011 at 9.30 a.m. for the purpose of having an account
laid before them showing the manner in which the winding-up has been conducted and the property of the company
disposed of and for hearing any explanation that may be given by the liquidator and also of determining by a special
resolution of the company by the shareholders, the manner in which the books of accounts and documents of the company
and of the liquidator shall be disposed of.
Nagercoil,
2nd March 2011.

JAYASHREE SRIDHAR,
Liquidator.
